
DROP TABLE LABEL;
DROP TABLE LABEL_TRANSLATION;
DROP TABLE LANGUAGE;

CREATE TABLE LANGUAGE (
	language_id NUMBER(10),
	language_code VARCHAR(45 CHAR),
	language_name VARCHAR(150 CHAR),
	date_modified DATE,
	date_added DATE);

CREATE TABLE LABEL (
	label_id NUMBER(10),
	label_code VARCHAR(45 CHAR),
	date_modified DATE,
	date_added DATE);

CREATE TABLE LABEL_TRANSLATION (
	label_translation_id NUMBER(10),
	label_id NUMBER(10),
	language_id NUMBER(10),
	label_translation_text VARCHAR(1000),
	date_modified DATE,
	date_added DATE);
